; Disassembly of the Sun 3/60 boot rom
; Version 1.9 -- image send to me by Dan and
; read out of a chip in one of his systems.
;
; Tom Trebisky  5-11-2025
;
; The ROM image is 64K (65536 bytes) in size.
; The last 16 bit word is a checksum.
;
; Some condensed notes on the m68k
; "motion" in the syntax is left to right, so
;   moveq #3,%d0 places 3 into the d0 register.
; This is exactly opposite from ARM where
; "motion" is from right to left, here:
;   movs    r0, #0  places the value 0 into r0

; ==========================================
; The first two words are read by the processor at reset
0fef0000:  0fe60c00		; stack pointer
0fef0004:  0fef00ee		; initial PC

; The rest of these are a "jump table" into various
;  places in the ROM
; I wonder what it means when the word begins
;    with ffff ?  Comparing to the Sun3-80 rom,
;    I see the same entries there begin with fef7
;    which is clearly not in the ROM space.

0fef0008:  0fef2d34
